Comprehensive Credit Spread Trading Framework:\n```python\nclass CreditSpreadTradingStrategy:\n    def __init__(\n        self, \n        notional_volume=200_000_000,\n        trade_parameters={\n            'entry_threshold': 2,\n            'exit_threshold': 0,\n            'bid_ask_spread': 0.0005  # 5 bps\n        }\n    ):\n        self.notional_volume = notional_volume\n        self.parameters = trade_parameters\n        \n        # Advanced signal generation and risk management\n        self.signal_generator = self.create_robust_signal_methodology()\n        self.risk_manager = self.develop_adaptive_risk_framework()\n    \n    def create_robust_signal_methodology(self):\n        class CreditSignalGenerator:\n            def __init__(self, rolling_window=50):\n                self.rolling_window = rolling_window\n            \n            def compute_advanced_spread_metrics(self, spread_data):\n                # Multi-dimensional spread analysis\n                def compute_metrics():\n                    return {\n                        'z_score': self.compute_z_score(spread_data),\n                        'hazard_rate_differential': self.compute_hazard_rate_diff(spread_data),\n                        'basis_trade_signal': self.analyze_cds_bond_basis(spread_data)\n                    }\n                \n                def compute_z_score(data):\n                    # Robust z-score computation\n                    ma = data.rolling(window=self.rolling_window).mean()\n                    std = data.rolling(window=self.rolling_window).std()\n                    \n                    # Winsorized z-score to reduce false signals\n                    z_score = (data - ma) / std\n                    return winsorize_z_score(z_score)\n                \n                def compute_hazard_rate_diff(data):\n                    # Advanced hazard rate differential\n                    def estimate_hazard_rate(spread_series):\n                        # Implement survival probability estimation\n                        # Using parametric or non-parametric methods\n                        return survival_probability_estimate(spread_series)\n                    \n                    hazard_rates = {\n                        'current': estimate_hazard_rate(data),\n                        'historical': estimate_historical_hazard_rate(data)\n                    }\n                    \n                    return compute_hazard_rate_differential(hazard_rates)\n                \n                def analyze_cds_bond_basis(data):\n                    # Comprehensive basis trade analysis\n                    def compute_basis_metrics():\n                        cds_spreads = extract_cds_spreads(data)\n                        bond_spreads = extract_bond_spreads(data)\n                        \n                        return {\n                            'basis_spread': cds_spreads - bond_spreads,\n                            'liquidity_adjustment': estimate_liquidity_premium()\n                        }\n                    \n                    basis_metrics = compute_basis_metrics()\n                    return evaluate_basis_trade_signal(basis_metrics)\n                \n                return compute_metrics()\n            \n            def generate_trade_signal(self, spread_data):\n                # Advanced multi-factor signal generation\n                metrics = self.compute_advanced_spread_metrics(spread_data)\n                \n                def combine_signals():\n                    # Weighted signal combination\n                    signal_weights = {\n                        'z_score': 0.4,\n                        'hazard_rate': 0.3,\n                        'basis_trade': 0.3\n                    }\n                    \n                    combined_signal = (\n                        metrics['z_score'] * signal_weights['z_score'] +\n                        metrics['hazard_rate_differential'] * signal_weights['hazard_rate'] +\n                        metrics['basis_trade_signal'] * signal_weights['basis_trade']\n                    )\n                    \n                    return combined_signal\n                \n                return combine_signals()\n        \n        return CreditSignalGenerator()\n    \n    def develop_adaptive_risk_framework(self):\n        class CreditRiskManager:\n            def __init__(self, trade_parameters):\n                self.parameters = trade_parameters\n            \n            def compute_optimal_thresholds(self, market_conditions):\n                # Dynamic threshold adaptation\n                def adjust_thresholds():\n                    base_entry = self.parameters['entry_threshold']\n                    base_exit = self.parameters['exit_threshold']\n                    \n                    # Adjust based on:\n                    # 1. Market volatility\n                    # 2. Liquidity conditions\n                    # 3. Systemic risk indicators\n                    \n                    volatility_adjustment = estimate_market_volatility()\n                    liquidity_penalty = compute_liquidity_discount()\n                    \n                    return {\n                        'entry_threshold': base_entry * (1 + volatility_adjustment),\n                        'exit_threshold': base_exit * (1 - liquidity_penalty)\n                    }\n                \n                return adjust_thresholds()\n            \n            def validate_trade_entry(self, signal, market_conditions):\n                # Comprehensive trade entry validation\n                def entry_criteria():\n                    adaptive_thresholds = self.compute_optimal_thresholds(market_conditions)\n                    \n                    signal_meets_entry = (\n                        abs(signal) >= adaptive_thresholds['entry_threshold']\n                    )\n                    \n                    liquidity_check = validate_liquidity_conditions()\n                    systemic_risk_check = assess_systemic_risk()\n                    \n                    return (\n                        signal_meets_entry and \n                        liquidity_check and \n                        systemic_risk_check\n                    )\n                \n                return entry_criteria()\n        \n        return CreditRiskManager(self.parameters)\n    \n    def execute_credit_spread_trade(self, spread_data, market_conditions):\n        # Comprehensive trade execution strategy\n        def trade_workflow():\n            # Generate trading signal\n            signal = self.signal_generator.generate_trade_signal(spread_data)\n            \n            # Validate trade entry\n            trade_approved = self.risk_manager.validate_trade_entry(\n                signal, \n                market_conditions\n            )\n            \n            if trade_approved:\n                # Execute trade with adaptive sizing\n                return execute_credit_spread_trade(\n                    signal, \n                    self.notional_volume\n                )\n            else:\n                return None\n        \n        return trade_workflow()\n\n# Performance Simulation\ndef simulate_credit_spread_strategy():\n    strategy = CreditSpreadTradingStrategy(\n        notional_volume=200_000_000,\n        trade_parameters={\n            'entry_threshold': 2,\n            'exit_threshold': 0,\n            'bid_ask_spread': 0.0005\n        }\n    )\n    \n    # Monte Carlo simulation of credit spread trading\n    performance_metrics = run_credit_spread_simulation(strategy)\n    return performance_metrics\n```\n\nKey Strategy Recommendations:\n1. Principal components analysis for factor neutralization\n                def compute_principal_portfolios():\n                    # Compute factor correlation matrix\n                    factor_corr = np.corrcoef(returns.T)\n                    \n                    # Eigendecomposition\n                    eigenvalues, eigenvectors = np.linalg.eig(factor_corr)\n                    \n                    # Select principal components\n                    principal_components = eigenvectors[:, np.argsort(eigenvalues)[::-1]]\n                    \n                    # Identify statistically significant factor drifts\n                    drift_stats = estimate_factor_drift()\n                    significant_drift = drift_stats[drift_stats > 2 * drift_stats.std()]\n                    \n                    return significant_drift\n                \n                def hedge_factor_drift():\n                    # Implement dynamic hedging\n                    significant_drifts = detect_significant_drift()\n                    \n                    hedge_weights = -significant_drifts / significant_drifts.sum()\n                    return hedge_weights\n                \n                return hedge_factor_drift()\n        \n        return DynamicHedgingModule()\n    \n    def execute_momentum_strategy(self, returns):\n        # Advanced factor model configuration\n        self.risk_model = self.create_enhanced_risk_model(risk_model)\n        self.optimization_framework = self.develop_robust_optimization_strategy()\n        self.stability_handler = self.implement_factor_stability_mechanisms()\n    \n    def create_enhanced_risk_model(self, base_model):\n        # Advanced risk model construction\n        class EnhancedRiskModel:\n            def __init__(self, model_type):\n                self.model_type = model_type\n                self.factor_library = self.build_comprehensive_factor_library()\n            \n            def build_comprehensive_factor_library(self):\n                # Extensive factor collection\n                def core_factors():\n                    return [\n                        'market_risk',\n                        'size',\n                        'value',\n                        'momentum',\n                        'quality',\n                        'investment',\n                        'profitability'\n                    ]\n                \n                def alternative_factors():\n                    return [\n                        'sentiment',\n                        'liquidity',\n                        'earnings_momentum',\n                        'balance_sheet_strength',\n                        'competitive_advantage'\n                    ]\n                \n                def market_regime_factors():\n                    return [\n                        'volatility_regime',\n                        'market_sentiment',\n                        'economic_cycle_indicator'\n                    ]\n                \n                return {\n                    'core': core_factors(),\n                    'alternative': alternative_factors(),\n                    'regime_dependent': market_regime_factors()\n                }\n            \n            def compute_factor_covariance(self, returns_data):\n                # Advanced covariance matrix estimation\n                def ledoit_wolf_shrinkage():\n                    # Robust covariance matrix estimation\n                    def ledoit_wolf_estimator(X):\n                        # Implement Ledoit-Wolf shrinkage\n                        n_samples, n_features = X.shape\n                        \n                        # Compute sample covariance\n                        sample_cov = np.cov(X, rowvar=False)\n                        \n                        # Compute shrinkage intensity\n                        def estimate_shrinkage_intensity():\n                            # Compute optimal shrinkage parameter\n                            beta_hat = np.trace(sample_cov)**2 / (n_samples * np.sum(sample_cov**2))\n                            return min(max(beta_hat, 0), 1)\n                        \n                        shrinkage_intensity = estimate_shrinkage_intensity()\n                        \n                        # Shrinkage target (identity matrix)\n                        identity_cov = np.eye(n_features) * np.trace(sample_cov) / n_features\n                        \n                        # Compute shrunk covariance\n                        shrunk_cov = (1 - shrinkage_intensity) * sample_cov + \\\n                                     shrinkage_intensity * identity_cov\n                        \n                        return shrunk_cov\n                    \n                    return ledoit_wolf_estimator(returns_data)\n                \n                def near_positive_definite_projection():\n                    # Ensure positive definiteness\n                    def higham_nearest_correlation(A):\n                        # Higham's algorithm for nearest correlation matrix\n                        def is_positive_definite(X):\n                            try:\n                                np.linalg.cholesky(X)\n                                return True\n                            except np.linalg.LinAlgError:\n                                return False\n                        \n                        # Iterative projection\n                        X = A.copy()\n                        Y = A.copy()\n                        iter_count = 0\n                        max_iter = 100\n                        \n                        while not is_positive_definite(X) and iter_count < max_iter:\n                            # Symmetrization\n                            R = X - Y\n                            X_k = (X + X.T) / 2\n                            \n                            # Nearest correlation matrix\n                            D = np.diag(1 / np.sqrt(np.diag(X_k)))\n                            X = D @ X_k @ D\n                            \n                            # Project back\n                            X = (X + X.T) / 2\n                            iter_count += 1\n                        \n                        return X\n                    \n                    return higham_nearest_correlation(ledoit_wolf_shrinkage())\n                \n                # Combine techniques\n                covariance_matrix = near_positive_definite_projection()\n                return covariance_matrix\n            \n            def factor_pca_decomposition(self, covariance_matrix):\n                # Principal Component Analysis for factor reduction\n                def compute_principal_components():\n                    # Eigendecomposition of covariance matrix\n                    eigenvalues, eigenvectors = np.linalg.eig(covariance_matrix)\n                    \n                    # Sort eigenvalues in descending order\n                    sorted_indices = np.argsort(eigenvalues)[::-1]\n                    eigenvalues = eigenvalues[sorted_indices]\n                    eigenvectors = eigenvectors[:, sorted_indices]\n                    \n                    # Compute explained variance\n                    total_variance = np.sum(eigenvalues)\n                    cumulative_variance_ratio = np.cumsum(eigenvalues) / total_variance\n                    \n                    # Select principal components\n                    num_components = np.argmax(cumulative_variance_ratio >= 0.95) + 1\n                    \n                    return {\n                        'principal_components': eigenvectors[:, :num_components],\n                        'explained_variance_ratio': cumulative_variance_ratio[:num_components]\n                    }\n                \n                return compute_principal_components()\n        \n        return EnhancedRiskModel(base_model)\n    \n    def develop_robust_optimization_strategy(self):\n        # Advanced portfolio optimization\n        class PortfolioOptimizationModule:\n            @staticmethod\n            def compute_transaction_costs(trades, market_data):\n                # Advanced transaction cost estimation\n                def market_impact_model():\n                    # Adaptive transaction cost estimation\n                    def compute_market_impact(trade_size, liquidity):\n                        # Non-linear market impact function\n                        # Consider stock size, liquidity, and trading volume\n                        market_impact_coefficient = estimate_market_impact_coefficient(\n                            trade_size, \n                            liquidity\n                        )\n                        \n                        return market_impact_coefficient * trade_size\n                    \n                    # Separate small and large cap transaction costs\n                    def small_cap_adjustment(trades):\n                        # Higher transaction cost for less liquid stocks\n                        small_cap_penalty = 1.5  # 50% higher cost\n                        return trades * small_cap_penalty\n                    \n                    return small_cap_adjustment(\n                        compute_market_impact(trades, market_data['liquidity'])\n                    )\n                \n                def implementation_shortfall():\n                    # Compute execution slippage\n                    def estimate_slippage(trades, market_data):\n                        # Consider:\n                        # 1. Bid-ask spread\n                        # 2. Intraday price movement\n                        # 3. Execution timing\n                        \n                        spread_cost = market_data['bid_ask_spread'] * trades\n                        price_movement_cost = estimate_price_movement_impact(\n                            trades, \n                            market_data\n                        )\n                        \n                        return spread_cost + price_movement_cost\n                    \n                    return estimate_slippage(trades, market_data)\n                \n                # Combine multiple transaction cost models\n                market_impact = market_impact_model()\n                implementation_shortfall_cost = implementation_shortfall()\n                \n                return market_impact + implementation_shortfall_cost\n            \n            def regime_switching_optimization(self, market_regime):\n                # Adaptive optimization based on market regime\n                def compute_regime_dependent_weights():\n                    # Adjust factor weights based on market conditions\n                    regime_weight_map = {\n                        'low_volatility': {\n                            'momentum_weight': 1.2,\n                            'quality_weight': 0.8,\n                            'value_weight': 1.0\n                        },\n                        'high_volatility': {\n                            'momentum_weight': 0.7,\n                            'quality_weight': 1.3,\n                            'value_weight': 1.5\n                        },\n                        'neutral': {\n                            'momentum_weight': 1.0,\n                            'quality_weight': 1.0,\n                            'value_weight': 1.0\n                        }\n                    }\n                    \n                    return regime_weight_map.get(\n                        market_regime, \n                        regime_weight_map['neutral']\n                    )\n                \n                def constrained_optimization():\n                    # Regime-dependent portfolio optimization\n                    # Use quadratic programming with regime-specific constraints\n                    regime_weights = compute_regime_dependent_weights()\n                    \n                    return solve_quadratic_optimization(\n                        objective_function,\n                        constraints,\n                        regime_weights\n                    )\n                \n                return constrained_optimization()\n        \n        return PortfolioOptimizationModule()\n    \n    def implement_factor_stability_mechanisms(self):\n        # Factor stability and temporal analysis\n        class FactorStabilityHandler:\n            def detect_factor_regime_shifts(self, factor_returns):\n                # Detect significant changes in factor behavior\n                def compute_regime_change_indicators():\n                    # Use multiple techniques to detect regime shifts\n                    def cusum_change_point_detection():\n                        # Cumulative sum change point detection\n                        cusum_statistic = compute_cusum(factor_returns)\n                        return detect_regime_change(cusum_statistic)\n                    \n                    def bayesian_regime_detection():\n                        # Bayesian approach to regime identification\n                        regime_probabilities = compute_regime_probabilities(factor_returns)\n                        return identify_regime_shifts(regime_probabilities)\n                    \n                    def statistical_test_battery():\n                        # Compute transaction costs for proposed trades\n            proposed_trades = portfolio_construction()['portfolio_weights']\n            \n            transaction_costs = self.optimization_framework.compute_transaction_costs(\n                proposed_trades,\n                market_data\n            )\n            \n            return transaction_costs\n        \n        # Integrate all components\n        optimization_result = portfolio_construction()\n        optimization_result['transaction_costs'] = transaction_cost_estimation()\n        \n        return optimization_result\n\n# Performance Simulation\ndef simulate_multi_factor_optimization():\n    model = MultiFactorOptimizationModel(\n        risk_model='enhanced_axioma',\n        optimization_targets={\n            'factor_stability': 0.95,\n            'transaction_cost_accuracy': 0.9,\n            'risk_decomposition_quality': 0.95\n        }\n    )\n    \n    # Server Depreciation (Double-Declining Balance Method):\n```python\ndef double_declining_balance_depreciation(\n    initial_cost=50000, \n    salvage_value=5000, \n    useful_life=5\n):\n    # Compute annual depreciation using double-declining balance method\n    def calculate_depreciation_schedule():\n        # Compute depreciation rate\n        annual_rate = 2 / useful_life\n        \n        # Initialize variables\n        book_value = initial_cost\n        depreciation_schedule = []\n        \n        for year in range(1, useful_life + 1):\n            # Compute depreciation for the year\n            if book_value * annual_rate > book_value - salvage_value:\n                # Adjust final year to reach salvage value\n                year_depreciation = book_value - salvage_value\n            else:\n                year_depreciation = book_value * annual_rate\n            \n            # Update book value\n            book_value -= year_depreciation\n            \n            depreciation_schedule.append({\n                \'Year\': year,\n                \'Depreciation\': year_depreciation,\n                \'Book Value\': book_value\n            })\n        \n        return depreciation_schedule\n    \n    return calculate_depreciation_schedule()\n\n# Server Depreciation Results\nserver_depreciation = double_declining_balance_depreciation()\nprint("Server Depreciation Schedule (Double-Declining Balance):")\nfor entry in server_depreciation:\n    print(f"Year {entry[\'Year\']}: Depreciation = ${entry[\'Depreciation\']:.2f}, Book Value = ${entry[\'Book Value\']:.2f}")\n```\n\n2. Advanced environment configuration\n        self.market_data = market_data\n        self.config = config\n        \n        # State and action space definition\n        self.num_assets = market_data.shape[1]\n        self.state_history_length = 20  # Rolling window for state representation\n        \n        # Observation space: historical returns, momentum, volatility\n        self.observation_space = spaces.Box(\n            low=-np.inf, \n            high=np.inf, \n            shape=(self.num_assets * 3,), \n            dtype=np.float32\n        )\n        \n        # Action space: portfolio weights for each asset\n        self.action_space = spaces.Box(\n            low=-self.config[\'max_leverage\'], \n            high=self.config[\'max_leverage\'], \n            shape=(self.num_assets,), \n            dtype=np.float32\n        )\n        \n        # Environment state tracking\n        self.current_step = 0\n        self.portfolio_history = []\n        self.state_history = []\n    \n    def _compute_advanced_state(self):\n        # Comprehensive state representation\n        def extract_features():\n            # Rolling window features\n            window = self.market_data[max(0, self.current_step-self.state_history_length):self.current_step+1]\n            \n            # Feature extraction techniques\n            returns = window.pct_change().dropna()\n            \n            features = {\n                \'returns\': returns.mean(),\n                \'momentum\': self._compute_momentum(returns),\n                \'volatility\': self._compute_volatility(returns),\n                \'correlation\': self._compute_correlation(returns)\n            }\n            \n            return np.concatenate([\n                features[\'returns\'],\n                features[\'momentum\'],\n                features[\'volatility\']\n            ])\n        \n        def _compute_momentum(returns):\n            # Multi-factor momentum computation\n            return returns.rolling(window=10).mean() / returns.rolling(window=20).std()\n        \n        def _compute_volatility(returns):\n            # Advanced volatility estimation\n            return returns.rolling(window=10).std()\n        \n        def _compute_correlation(returns):\n            # Correlation-based feature extraction\n            return np.linalg.eigvals(returns.corr())\n        \n        return extract_features()\n    \n    def _compute_reward(self, portfolio_weights, next_returns):\n        # Transaction cost penalization\n            def compute_transaction_costs():\n                # Advanced transaction cost model\n                if len(self.portfolio_history) > 0:\n                    prev_weights = self.portfolio_history[-1]\n                    turnover = np.abs(portfolio_weights - prev_weights).sum()\n                    \n                    # Non-linear transaction cost function\n                    tc_penalty = (\n                        self.config[\'transaction_cost_rate\'] * \n                        (turnover ** 1.5)  # Non-linear scaling\n                    )\n                    \n                    return tc_penalty\n                return 0\n            \n            # Penalize downside risk\n                \'transaction_cost\': -transaction_cost\n            }\n            \n            # Weighted reward function\n            reward = (\n                0.5 * reward_components[\'return_component\'] +\n                0.3 * reward_components[\'risk_adjustment\'] +\n                0.2 * reward_components[\'transaction_cost\']\n            )\n            \n            return reward, metrics\n        \n        return compute_performance_metrics()\n    \n    def _compute_sharpe_ratio(self, weights, returns):\n        # Standard Sharpe ratio computation\n        portfolio_return = np.dot(weights, returns)\n        return (portfolio_return - self.config[\'risk_free_rate\']) / np.std(returns)\n    \n    def _compute_sortino_ratio(self, weights, returns):\n        # Sortino ratio: focuses on downside risk\n        portfolio_return = np.dot(weights, returns)\n        downside_returns = returns[returns < 0]\n        downside_deviation = np.std(downside_returns)\n        return (portfolio_return - self.config[\'risk_free_rate\']) / downside_deviation if downside_deviation > 0 else 0\n    \n    def _compute_calmar_ratio(self, weights, returns):\n        # Calmar ratio: considers maximum drawdown\n        portfolio_return = np.dot(weights, returns)\n        cumulative_returns = np.cumprod(1 + returns) - 1\n        max_drawdown = np.max(cumulative_returns - np.maximum.accumulate(cumulative_returns))\n        return portfolio_return / abs(max_drawdown) if max_drawdown < 0 else 0\n    \n    def step(self, action):\n        # Environment step function\n        if self.current_step >= len(self.market_data) - 1:\n            return None, 0, True, {}\n        \n        # Normalize and clip action\n        portfolio_weights = np.clip(action, -self.config[\'max_leverage\'], self.config[\'max_leverage\'])\n        portfolio_weights /= np.sum(np.abs(portfolio_weights))  # Advanced policy network\n        class PolicyNetwork(nn.Module):\n            def __init__(self, input_dim, output_dim):\n                super().__init__()\n                self.shared_layers = nn.Sequential(\n                    nn.Linear(input_dim, 128),\n                    nn.ReLU(),\n                    nn.BatchNorm1d(128),\n                    nn.Linear(128, 64),\n                    nn.ReLU(),\n                    nn.BatchNorm1d(64)\n                )\n                \n                self.policy_head = nn.Linear(64, output_dim)\n                self.value_head = nn.Linear(64, 1)\n            \n            def forward(self, x):\n                features = self.shared_layers(x)\n                policy_logits = self.policy_head(features)\n                value = self.value_head(features)\n                return policy_logits, value\n        \n        return PolicyNetwork(\n            input_dim=env.observation_space.shape[0], \n            output_dim=env.action_space.shape[0]\n        )\n    \n    def train(self, num_episodes=100):\n        # Advanced PPO training algorithm\n        for episode in range(num_episodes):\n            state = self.env.reset()\n            done = False\n            episode_rewards = []\n            \n            while not done:\n                #
